CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS Warehouses (warehouse_id INT PRIMARY KEY, warehouse_location STRING, warehouse_capacity INT);</t><s>UPDATE Products SET product_price = 25.99 WHERE product_id = 201;</s>
